msg:Just finished a five night stay at The Regent Chongqing, was one of the best hotel experiences ever.  

Arrived at the start of the national three day Duanwu Dragon Boat Festival and was warmly greeted with two tasty green bean cake pastries in a traditional wood basket as a welcome amenity in the room.

Breakfast has an abundance of options, everything fresh and delicious.  

Ate at the third floor Chinese restaurant twice and the dishes there are truly outstanding, some of the best tasting dishes I‚Äôve ever tasted in Sichuan province and also rated as the second best restaurant in Chongqing on this website.  Compared to some of the top tier restaurants in cities like Beijing and Shanghai, also very reasonably priced and affordable. 

What‚Äôs really nice is the hotel offers complimentary laundry service for up to three pieces per day which I thought was a very thoughtful service.  Mini bar in hotel room also completely free and restocked daily.  Water pressure in room‚Äôs shower was also very strong which made showering very enjoyable.  

Hospitality is really on another level here.  During the stay I experienced:

-	A small soft cloth wipe was left next to my laptop since the staff noticed my laptop screen was a bit dirty
-	Staff during breakfast would go out of there way to ask if I wanted or needed assistance in preparing a bowl of noodles, per my request they kindly prepared one for me with the most popular condiments used by locals
-	One of the chefs during breakfast made it known if there was anything at all I wanted him to specially prepare for me he would gladly do it
-	Same chef (Mr. Swong), when he found out I would be departing for a day trip the next morning from the hotel at a very early hour (earlier than when the hotel breakfast dining would be open) made it be known that he would make arrangements for the hotel to prepare a bag of anything I wanted from the breakfast buffet to take with me so I could eat it in the car.  Sure enough, the next morning at the front desk reception there was a bag waiting for me containing various fresh fruit, a hard boiled egg, sticky rice, orange juice, banana, water, utensils.  When I walked outside to the car that had arrived to pick me up, both the driver and tour guide remarked they had never seen a hotel ever do this for a guest and that this must be a really exceptional hotel.
-	A complimentary bowl of fresh fruit was delivered and left in my room 
-	Upon check-out, received an immaculately wrapped gift box of Chongqing Small Noodles (dried, uncooked) which was accompanied by a specially prepared locally made peppercorn noodle sauce (wrapped in plastic), was actually the perfect gift since my Mom loves noodles and to see her face so happy and joyful upon receiving this gift brought me much happiness

Everywhere in the hotel, from the hotel front desk staff, the bellboys and staff working outside the front door, the staff at the 7th floor bar, the staff at the breakfast dining, to the staff on the 3rd floor Chinese restaurant, was treated so warmly and courteously and staff so helpful and thoughtful too.  

Victoria was especially gracious and helpful as when I arrived, I didn‚Äôt know where to eat and after asking me a few questions with regards to my tastes and kind of ambiance I would like in a restaurant, she recommended a very popular local Chongqing Hot Pot restaurant just a few minutes away.  This turned out to be great recommendation as the flavor of the hot pot was really great and the environment was more of a ‚Äòhole in the wall‚Äô place, very raucous and rowdy, just what I was looking for.  She would also periodically check in to see if everything was going okay and if there was anything she could assist with.  Will always be grateful to Victoria and the staff at Regent Chongqing for making my first trip to Chongqing so unforgettable and full of wonderful memories.

msg:I stayed at Chongqing Regent Hotel for 4 nights in mid-May. I felt very comfortable and the service was excellent. Highly recommended.

What we like
- The waiters at the front door and counter are very friendly and considerate.
- We have several couriers, and they all take the initiative to deliver them to the room and provide scissors to open the couriers.
- Breakfast is very rich, including bread, drinks, noodles, and scrambled eggs. Benedy will help bring them to your table. There are fruits and even mangoes~ If you don‚Äôt have time to eat, you can pack a small portion to eat on the road.
- The mini bar in the room is a special snack of Chongqing, so you don‚Äôt have to think about buying any souvenirs.
- The most touching and unexpected thing is that the hotel can provide some small supplies for free, such as humidifier/mosquito repellent/hair clips/mouthwash/steam eye mask/makeup remover wipes/hair straightener, etc. It is really considerate.
- The butler cabinet is really easy to use and you are not afraid of the embarrassment of opening the door.
- Will take the initiative to deliver takeaways
- The laundry service is very good. The clothes are returned folded and look like new. There is butter paper placed in the transparent bag. They will also check the clothes first.
- Postcards and stamps are included (I had a hard time finding them at tourist attractions before)
- If you are bored in the room, you can borrow board games like Monopoly to play
- There are flower petals in the bath and bubble bath is optional (menu in the picture is attached)
- There are a range of pillows to choose from, including soft, medium and hard, so there is always something suitable for you.
- Turndown service available
- There are a series of luxury brands offering in-store discounts or consumption discounts at ifs. We went to La Prairie for hand care, and we went to Ole to pick up a piece of bread. We can eat it when taking the high-speed rail.
- On the morning of check-out, the front desk called specifically to ask when it would be convenient to help us pick up our luggage. The guy came 10 minutes earlier than the scheduled time and was unwilling to make us wait. As it turned out, we were not ready yet. He even offered to help pack up hahahaha.
- The classic king-size bed room we booked with two breakfasts was really worth it no matter how expensive it was (my girlfriend was heartbroken at first and after staying there, she said she didn‚Äôt regret it at all for the price). I have stayed in other 5-star hotels in China before. (Guangzhou Four Seasons Shenzhen Ritz-Carlton Shanghai Langham, etc.) This time the Chongqing Regent‚Äôs real hotel ceiling
- We missed a few small items when we were carrying our luggage. The hotel called us to remind us and even helped us send them back by courier. Thank you very much to the hotel.

Suggested points for improvement
(We really thought hard to come up with some things we could fault)
- There is no "please clean now" reminder light/sign in the room
- We have two large suitcases and there is not enough space in the cloakroom, but the hotel does not have luggage racks to borrow.
- We borrowed a humidifier but there were not enough plugs in the room. We wanted to put it near the window but didn‚Äôt know where to put it (we might be able to borrow a mopboard but we didn‚Äôt ask)
- Boxing bags are not provided in the fitness room
- It would be better if you add more fruits to the minibar every day
- Please tell me if the room window is a one-way mirror

Thank you very much for the wonderful service of Regent Hotel, which allowed us to enjoy a pleasant and warm stay in Chongqing. Finally, friends, please have an appreciation attitude and never take it for granted. If you have the opportunity to come to Chongqing next time, you will definitely stay at your hotel again.

This time we booked a river view room and a city view room, the river view is very beautiful~ The package we purchased includes 3 times of Liangjiang Bar consumption (recommended experience!), we only used it twice, and the hotel gave us a 9-space package (snacks + champagneüçæ)~

6. The washbasin is equipped with Baisuishan mineral water, as well as facial masks, sleep eye masks, and hot pot deodorizer (will be delivered to the room if you call)
7. Breakfast juice can be squeezed on the spot (fried dumplings and baked salmon head are particularly delicious, and the baby also likes it)

Service details
1. We want to wash the baby's eating pocket clothes after the meal , the restaurant staff took the initiative to help clean and dry it and send it back (it was very considerate to dry it, we can store it directly)

3. Three pieces of laundry service per person per day, children are also allowed, no additional charge
4. We hand-washed the baby vest and hung it on the wall. When we came back in the evening, the housekeeping staff had added a clothes drying rack and hung it up, and laid a blanket on the floor to prevent moisture
7. The data cable and the baby pajamas placed on the bedside were all organized
8. The bathroom door was laid with a non-slip mat
9. Shopping takeaways, the hotel staff delivered directly to the room
10. The noodles were ordered for breakfast, and they were cooked and delivered directly to the location, so guests don‚Äôt need to run back to pick them up

About room type
Book a river view room directly if the budget is sufficient
If you just come back to rest at night, you can consider the city view room with the Liangjiang Bar package (the biggest problem with the city view room is that it is too close to the opposite office building). There are discount packages on various platforms from time to time, which can be purchased first and then booked
City view room upgraded to river view room +466 per day

Compared with the stay in 21 years, it feels that the housekeeping staff is a bit tight this time. Last time we had a bubble bath, the staff directly filled the water for us; this time, they gave us sea salt or something, and then filled the water for us after we asked. Maybe they were too busy because there were too many guests staying recently.

Based on the overall experience, Regent is indeed a benchmark in the entire southwest hotel market. The entire polite and gentle corporate character always gives people a sense of moisturizing and quiet delicacy during the stay. If I were to choose it in Chongqing , Regent must be my first choice

Bedside lamps, sofa lampshades, decorative paintings, etc. are not dusty
From the hotel reception to the room service is just right
‚ÄãIt is particularly commendable that the hotel reflects the local culture of Chongqing
The free water and wine in the mini bar is fully equipped. The appearance of Chongqing‚Äôs local beverage Tianfu Cola is a good plus point. The additional Jiugongge snacks with Chongqing characteristics (Hechuan peach slices, dried croissant tofu, brown sugar, beef ****y, Crispy chili, strange-flavored beans, peanut crisps, rice candy, twist) are all accompanied by corresponding text introductions
The oil tea, small noodles, and tofu brain for breakfast can also allow guests from other places to experience Chongqing's street food without leaving home.
The little guests are also taken care of. The image of the little dinosaur that appeared on the children's slippers and children's bathrobes finally revealed the answer in the small gift bag given to the children when they left the store (this Chongqing dragon named Jingzi makes the little friends remember deeply)[ snicker]
Slight shortcomings are as follows
1. The basic rooms have no view at all, and the Niccolo at the same price is slightly better in the view of most rooms
2. The Benedict and waffles made for breakfast are slightly less delicate, but the taste of Benedict is worth 9.5 points
3. Under the circumstance that the traffic of breakfast is not large, the speed of the waiter to clear the empty plate feels a little lag.
4. The most unfortunate problem is that there is a lot of dust on the Tianfu Coke bottle in the mini bar in the guest room, and there is a bottle of mineral water in the bathroom that the previous guest opened and drank a sip of mineral water, which was not found and replaced by the cleaning staff. The housekeeper gave the solution in time and sent extra snacks and drinks in the room, which will still have an impact on the overall experience. I hope it is just an occasional phenomenon.
Summarize
From room to service to local experience, Regent is undoubtedly the best hotel in the main city of Chongqing
Regardless of landscape conditions, Regent should be the first choice

Of course, if you are particularly concerned about the landscape and less concerned about the service experience, Niccolo should be more suitable.
